class="elementor-widget-container">  <p>OUR CURRICULUM APPROACH</p> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-dfc9a13 elementor-widget__width-initial elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="dfc9a13" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container"> <h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Nurturing talents through multiple intelligence</h2> </div> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-92f129c e-con-full e-flex e-con e-child" data-id="92f129c" data-element_type="container" data-settings="{&quot;content_width&quot;:&quot;full&quot;}"> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-e4c2771 elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-id="e4c2771" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="text-editor.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container"> <p>At My Little Kingdom Preschool, we believe that each child is unique with his or her talents. Some are good with language, some are good at music or with people skills. By allowing your child to excel in their individual unique way, it will be a great confidence booster for them to excel.&nbsp;</p> <p class="nitro-offscreen">We follow a curriculum based on the all-encompassing principles of Howard Gardnerâ€™s Theory of Multiple Intelligence. This approach recognises eight distinct intelligences based on a childâ€™s natural ability and inclination.</p> </div> </div> </div> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element
